First time eating here and while my order was not completely correct (ordered half mushroom and black olives online and entire pizza had olives and mushrooms) which I think was more of an online error it was still a REALLY good pizza. Great flavor, cooked just right. Cheesey garlic bread wasn't greasy. Delivery was very timely and when we called about the error the young lady was very helpful on the phone. Prices aren't bad either, got a large 4 topping pizza and bread sticks and it was under $25 and that included tax, delivery fee and 20% tip. We will be ordering again!< /Review>

1546196154675< /date>
< rate>
4< /rate>
<review>This trail is an absolutely beautiful scenic route. You can see Vistas not only of Lake Chabot to the east but to the west you could actually see the San Francisco skyline along with Brisbane all the way to San Mateo Bridge. The only thing that would make this Trail better would be public restrooms-- there are none. I love being able to take my dog here to go walking off leash, which is allowed and clearly indicated by signs at the beginning of the path. It's also nice that the hours are 5am-10pm, meaning you can still go even when the days are short.

There is one main paved walking path heading up the middle of the ridge and several some dirt trails that run parallel and intersect the main path at times. Nice to have options since this is a regular spot for me and the doggo.

Only reason I knocked a star off is because of some of the other dog owners who leave used 💩 bags all over the place. Or even worse, don't even try and pick up! It's so frustrating. Please don't do this if you come with a dog. There is a trash can at the gate you can toss it into. Even if you pick it up on the way out (which clearly is not always the case...), it's not appropriate. Other walkers shouldn't have to look at/avoid/ignore/smell or otherwise be aware of a used 💩 bag on the ground. Like I said, I have a dog. I bring her here all the time. I understand it sucks to carry a used bag with you, but it's your dog and it's your responsibility! Pick that 💩 up and take it with you. End rant.</Text></record>

A local favorite which also caters to tourists, this deli offers a wide range of sandwiches and salads within a chic gift shop.  Come for the outdoor patio seating in back.  Your meal and conversation may be interrupted by either the aggressive birds or a train blasting past the property 30 feet from your table.  I recommend the turkey meatloaf sandwich.</Review>

< text>
We kept passing by this place as we walked through Berkeley and I kept saying how cute it was. We ended up staying around for dinner and decided to check this place out. We got the Middle Eastern plate which I love because I love sampling different things and this dish allows you to do that. It came with chicken cilica, Grecian spinach & feta sandwich, lamb lule, lemon chicken soup. The lemon chicken soup is delicious. I’m glad I chose that over the potato options. Everything else was pretty good, but nothing really stood out as a favorite. We also got the pomegranate chicken and that was really good with moist and tender pieces of chicken and good flavor.

Overall, it was a cute place and we were lucky to have a nice day so we could sit on the patio. The food is alright, but I like the variety.<//text>

<resp>None<//resp>< review>
It's been a while since I last visited Cafe La Med in Berkeley and ordered take-out of my favorite - pomegranate chicken. Sadly, since they were sold, the quality is not what it was. In the past you would get a little piece of cheese, a little piece of banana and a little piece of pineapple along with the entre. These were all missing. You also got hummus with a little slice of carrot and some full pieces of pita. This order had little pieces of pita that might as well have been white sandwich bread. The hummus came in a little plastic container and had very little flavor. I ordered the potato salad, which was OK, as the side which was slapped into a separate cardboard box. The menu has obviously changed for the worse. The chicken and rice overpowered with sweetness with not much finesse. Perhaps you get what I used to expect if you eat at the restaurant. Perhaps the lack of the little niceties is for money savings. I’d be happy to pay a few bucks more to get back my delicious chicken pomegranate of old.</review>

< Review>
Berkeley, College Ave location of a small chain of Bay Area Mediterranean restaurants with three additional locations in San Francisco. Good menu selection, and a plus for vegetarians and vegans is that they have a separate veggie menu. Notwithstanding that, the food was disappointingly average. Menu variety is good, prices are extremely reasonable. Service was so so, but it wasn't busy and my date and I sat and talked for over two hours. No one brought a check or pressed us to leave, so there were definitely some redeeming features. I could actually give them three and a half stars if there were such a choice. To get more, the food, service, and decor would have to be upgraded. Recommended if you are not expecting a gourmet meal.</Review>

I have eaten at La Mediteranee twice since it was recently sold. Sadly, the quality of the food is not the same.  The filo spinach rolls are not as light and crispy as they were for years.  The spinach filling is heavy and too moist. The vegetarian soup of which I've had two different ones, a lentil and a mushroom cream, were not good.  I did not finish either. And heavy cream cuts out vegans.  I hope the new owners make adjustments back to the old recipes because Le Med has been a favorite for me and many others for years and years.< /Review>

<rating>4< /rating>< review>
I must admit that I don’t enjoy Bay Area getting more and more expensive every day. When I go out I want to enjoy my time. La Méditerranée is a cozy place with Lebanese cuisine and moderately priced. A big appetizer, half liter of wine and desert cost us $40 without the tip. I had Datil Amandra which I got full just by looking at it. It’s so rich and tasty I’m positive that one person can never finish it. You have to give it a try tho since it’s so authentic. Also, you’ll never go wrong with the house wine. Just make sure you drink responsibly if you’re driving 🚘
If you can try and get a table in the patio. It’s darker and louder inside.< /review>

< review>
Went to La Mediterranee last night with my sister and friend. I've been to the location in Pac Heights and the menu seems different to me at the Berkeley location. We ordered the large sample platter to share, which was good. It included hummus, wrapped grape leaves, pita bread, tabbouleh and a few other items. For our mains my sister got the pomegranate chicken and I had the sampler platter, so I could try a variety of things. Everything was good but nothing exactly stood out or wowed me. I prefer the Pac Heights location in San Francisco, but this is a good option. They have outdoor seating as well which is nice on days with beautiful weather.<//review>

< user_id>
117337714919198286164< /user_id>
< text>
Very consistent food, casual atmosphere, okay service.  A favorite for 15+ years.  Way better than the San Francisco locations. Middle eastern plate, chicken pomegranate, filo dough plates are the favorites.  The kebabs are not very interesting and a bit on the dry side, so don't order those. Love the variety of food you get on the middle eastern plate and you can sub out an item for another item already on the dish (common sub-- Levant sandwich for a pomegranate chicken drumstick, or a filo dough piece). Favorite filo dough pieces: spinach and feta (Greek spanakopita) and chicken Cilicia (moroccan bisteeya). Date dessert is out of this world if you love medjool dates or even if you don't think you do.<//text>

< Text>
I would like to say Thank you very much to Kevin, Anna and Krishna at Action Urgent Care, Blossom Hill location. They were so kind and nice when I walked in unexpectedly on Sept 27, 2019 (a Friday evening) & requested copies of my records including all my health diaries which had always been scanned into the computer before or after my appointment visits; I explained I was flying out soon. This was not the location I had received my care from for over a year but it was the closest one to me where I was temporarily staying. I explained that during my move out of state several boxes were lost which included copies of medical records & written diaries regarding my injury. I waited a couple of hours but it was difficult to complete this task because of patients. They suggested I return the next day instead of waiting & that they would continue to copy as time allowed that night and staff would finish the next day if necessary & I could pick up then. I couldn't believe that they would staple the pages of each encounter together which took more time but I was told that's how he would want it done if he was picking up his records, so very considerate & thoughtful! I returned the next day, Saturday, late afternoon on the 28th, they were very busy again, yet continued to copy my records (team effort again) in between patients as I waited. Even the physician wonder what was happening when he saw me sitting and looking through my papers trying to make sure I had all my dates, he was very pleasant & understanding also. During this time your staff never neglected new walk-ins and prioritized those patients which I completely understood & would expect if I didn't feel well and required treatment. A few times, I realized a couple of diaries associated with some appointment dates were missing and they took the time to search the computer again & found those diary records finally & printed for me along with the others.
I appreciate their professionalism, teamwork, and never appearing that I was interfering with their day or adding work for them (I certainly had) especially when I had never been a patient at the Blossom Hill location. The location also very clean, spacious, and well-lit.</Text>

My son had to wait a couple of hours to see a Nurse Practitioner for a routine sports injury on a Saturday.  Somebody dropped the ball and I had to nag the staff by phone to send the script to Walgreens electronically after driving over and waiting 30 min in line at the pharmacy.

In principle NPs are great!  By using NPs a healthcare organization is supposed to be able to provide care without the high cost and long wait of a traditional practice.  In this case the cost was pretty high and the wait was pretty long so I feel like Action management is maximizing shareholder value rather than anything else.  Next time I will probably go to Samaritan Urgent Care which I have used in the past.  That way I can wait a long time to see a physician!< /text>

I just recently moved to San Jose and needed to see a doctor right away for pain in my right ear.  On 11/28/16 I called Urgent Care to see if I could stop by at noon to see a doctor.  Upon arrival I was welcomed by a nice young man at the front desk.  He gave me the registration forms to complete which didn't take long.  I waited approximately 15 minutes before a very nice nurse, professional and courteous came and directed me to an examining room to  speak with me about my illness.
